### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 89 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Survey Results\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|}\hlineAnswer & Percent \\\hlineNever & $31.3 \%$ \\\hlineRarely & $24.3 \%$ \\\hlineOften & $13.5 \%$ \\\hlineAlways & $30.9 \%$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows the results of a survey in which tablet users were asked how often they would watch video advertisements in order to access streaming content for free. Based on the table, which of the following is closest to the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never"?
Choices:
  A: 0.31
  B: 0.38
  C: 0.45
  D: 0.69
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We want to find the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never."
  We can use the formula for conditional probability: P(A|B) = P(A and B) / P(B).
  Let A be the event that a tablet user answered "Always" and B be the event that a tablet user did not answer "Never."
  We can find P(B) by adding the probabilities of "Rarely," "Often," and "Always."
  We can find P(A and B) by looking at the probability of "Always" and subtracting the probability of "Always" and "Never."
  Therefore, P(A|B) = (P(A and B) / P(B)) = ((0.309 - 0.313) / (0.243 + 0.135 + 0.309)) = 0.196 / 0.687 = 0.285.
  The closest choice to 0.285 is B: 0.38.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We want to find the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never."
  We can use the formula for conditional probability: P(A|B) = P(A and B) / P(B)
  Let A be the event that a tablet user answered "Always" and B be the event that a tablet user did not answer "Never."
  We can find P(A and B) by looking at the "Always" row and the non-"Never" columns, which add up to $30.9 \% + 13.5 \% = 44.4 \%$.
  We can find P(B) by looking at the non-"Never" rows, which add up to $24.3 \% + 13.5 \% + 30.9 \% = 68.7 \%$.
  Therefore, P(A|B) = P(A and B) / P(B) = 44.4 % / 68.7 % = 0.646, which is closest to 0.69.
  The answer is D: 0.69. 
Action: Answer("D")

  The probability of answering "Always" given that the tablet user did not answer "Never" is $\frac{30.9 \%}{68.7 \%} \approx 0.449$.
  The closest answer choice is C: 0.45.

Question: Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members for an upcoming project. The staff members will be made up of junior directors, who will be paid $\$ 640$ per week, and senior directors, who will be paid $\$ 880$ per week. Her budget for paying the staff members is no more than $\$ 9,700$ per week. She must hire at least 3 junior directors and at least 1 senior director. Which of the following systems of inequalities represents the conditions described if $x$ is the number of junior directors and $y$ is the number of senior directors?
Choices:
  A: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  B: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  C: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
  D: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$

  The number of junior directors should be greater than or equal to 3.
  $x \geq 3$

  $y \geq 1$

  $y \geq 1$ (she must hire at least 1 senior director)
  The correct answer is A: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$

  $640x + 880y \leq 9700$ (budget constraint)
  $x + y \geq 10$ (at least 10 staff members)
  $x \geq 3$ (at least 3 junior directors)
  $y \geq 1$ (at least 1 senior director)
  The correct answer is A.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 91 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$If $(x, y)$ is a solution to the system of equations above, what is the value of $x-y$ ?
Choices:
  A: -20
  B: $\quad-8$
  C: -4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can solve the system of equations by elimination method.
  Multiplying the first equation by $2$ and the second equation by $3$, we get:
  $$\begin{aligned}& 4 x-6 y=-28 \\& 9 x-6 y=-18\end{aligned}$$
  Subtracting the second equation from the first, we get:
  $$-5x=-10 \implies x=2$$
  Substituting $x=2$ in the second equation, we get:
  $$3(2)-2y=-6 \implies y=6$$
  Therefore, $(x,y)=(2,6)$ and $x-y=-4$.
  The answer is C: -4.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 92 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The equation of a line in slope-intercept form is $y = mx + b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  Since the line passes through the origin, the y-intercept is 0.
  Therefore, the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$.
  To check which point lies on the line, we can substitute the coordinates of each point into the equation of the line and see if the equation is true.
  Substituting $(0,7)$ gives $7 = \frac{1}{7}(0)$, which is not true.
  Substituting $(1,7)$ gives $7 = \frac{1}{7}(1)$, which is not true.
  Substituting $(7,7)$ gives $7 = \frac{1}{7}(7)$, which is true.
  Substituting $(14,2)$ gives $2 = \frac{1}{7}(14)$, which is not true.
  Therefore, the point $(7,7)$ lies on the line.
  The answer is C: $(7,7)$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The equation of a line passing through the origin with slope $m$ is $y = mx$.
  The slope of the line is $\frac{1}{7}$, so the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$.
  To check which point lies on the line, we can substitute the $x$ and $y$ values of each point into the equation of the line and see if the equation holds true.
  Substituting $(0,7)$ into the equation of the line gives $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 0 = 0$, which is not equal to 7.
  Substituting $(1,7)$ into the equation of the line gives $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 1 = \frac{1}{7}$, which is not equal to 7.
  Substituting $(7,7)$ into the equation of the line gives $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 7 = 1$, which is not equal to 7.
  Substituting $(14,2)$ into the equation of the line gives $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 14 = 2$, which is equal to 2.
  Therefore, the point $(14,2)$ lies on the line.
  The answer is D: $(14,2)$.
Action: Answer("D")

  The equation of a line passing through the origin with slope $m$ is given by $y = mx$.

  To check which point lies on the line, we can substitute the $x$ and $y$ coordinates of each point into the equation of the line and see if the equation is satisfied.
  For point A: $y = \frac{1}{7}x = \frac{1}{7}(0) = 0$, which is not equal to 7. Therefore, point A does not lie on the line.
  For point B: $y = \frac{1}{7}x = \frac{1}{7}(1) = \frac{1}{7}$, which is not equal to 7. Therefore, point B does not lie on the line.

  For point D: $y = \frac{1}{7}x = \frac{1}{7}(14) = 2$, which is not equal to 2. Therefore, point D does not lie on the line.
  Therefore, the point that lies on the line is C: $(7,7)$.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 93 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
  Therefore, the total number of calories from Super Grain cereal and Crunchy Grain cereal is 270.
  The number of calories from Super Grain cereal is $240x$.
  The number of calories from Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{210}{\frac{3}{4}}\left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right)-50$.
  We can solve for $x$ using the equation $240x+\frac{210}{\frac{3}{4}}\left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right)-50=270$.
  Solving for $x$ gives $x=\frac{1}{3}$.
  Therefore, Jennifer mixes $\frac{1}{3}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-\frac{1}{3}=\frac{1}{2}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The answer is $\frac{1}{3}$ cup.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4} - x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
  The total number of calories from Crunchy Grain cereal is $210 \times \frac{3}{4} = 157.5$.
  The total number of calories from Super Grain cereal is $240x$.
  Therefore, we can set up the following equation: $157.5 + 240x = 270$.
  Solving for $x$, we get $x = \frac{1}{4}$.
  Therefore, Jennifer mixes $\frac{1}{4}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4} - \frac{1}{4} = \frac{1}{2}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The answer is D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$.
Action: Answer("D")

  Let's assume that Jennifer will mix $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
  The total number of calories from Crunchy Grain cereal is $210 \times \frac{3}{4} \times \frac{50}{210} = \frac{225}{4}$.
  The total number of calories from Super Grain cereal is $240x$.
  Therefore, we can set up the following equation: $\frac{225}{4} + 240x = 270$.
  Solving for $x$, we get $x = \frac{3}{8}$.
  Therefore, Jennifer will mix $\frac{3}{8}$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-\frac{3}{8}=\frac{3}{8}$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{\frac{3}{8}}{1}=\frac{3}{8}$.
  The answer is $\frac{3}{8}$, which is equivalent to $\frac{1}{4}$.

  The number of calories from Super Grain cereal is 240x.
  The total number of calories is the sum of the calories from Crunchy Grain cereal and the calories from Super Grain cereal.

  The question asks for the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture, so we need to find the ratio of Super Grain cereal to the total mixture.
  The total amount of cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup $= \frac{9}{12}$ cup.
  Therefore, the ratio of Super Grain cereal to the total mixture is $\frac{1/3}{9/12}=\frac{4}{9}$.
  The amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{4}{9}\cdot 1=\frac{4}{9}$ cup.

Response 8:
Thought:
To solve the problem, we need to use the information given about the calories in each cereal and the total number of calories in the mixture. Let's start by finding the number of calories in one cup of Crunchy Grain cereal. Since a serving size is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, we can find the number of calories in one cup by multiplying both sides of the equation by $\frac{4}{3}$: 

$\frac{4}{3} \cdot 210 = 280$ calories in one cup of Crunchy Grain cereal.

Next, we can use the information about the total number of calories in the mixture to find the number of calories in one cup of Super Grain cereal. If one cup of the mixture has 270 calories and one cup of Crunchy Grain cereal has 280 calories, then one cup of Super Grain cereal must have:

$270 - 280 = -10$ calories in one cup of Super Grain cereal.

This doesn't make sense, so we need to adjust our approach. Let's try using a variable to represent the number of cups of Super Grain cereal in the mixture. If we let $x$ be the number of cups of Super Grain cereal, then the number of calories in one cup of the mixture can be expressed as:

$240x + 280(1-x) = 270$

Simplifying this equation, we get:

$-20x + 280 = 270$

$-20x = -10$

$x = \frac{1}{2}$

Therefore, the answer is D: $\frac{1}{2}$ cup.

Topic: Math
Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The equation gives the height of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet.
  We need to find $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$.
  Rearranging the given equation, we get $v t=h+k+16 t^{2}$.
  Dividing both sides by $t$, we get $v=\frac{h+k}{t}+16 t$.
  Therefore, the answer is D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The equation given is $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$.
  We need to isolate $v$ on one side of the equation.
  We can do that by adding $16t^2$ to both sides and then dividing by $t$.
  $h+k=16t^2+vt$
  $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16t$
  Therefore, the answer is C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16t$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
  The given equation is $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$.
  We need to find $v$ in terms of $h$, $t$, and $k$.
  Rearranging the given equation, we get $v t=h+k-16 t^{2}$.
  Dividing both sides by $t$, we get $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$.
  Therefore, the answer is C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$.
Action: Answer("C")

Thought:
  The equation given is $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$.
  To solve for $v$, we need to isolate $v$ on one side of the equation.
  We can do this by adding $16t^2$ and subtracting $k$ from both sides of the equation.
  This gives us $v t=h-16 t^{2}-k$.
  We can then divide both sides by $t$ to get $v=\frac{h-16 t^{2}-k}{t}$.
  Simplifying this expression gives us $v=\frac{h-k}{t}-16t$.
  Therefore, the answer is D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t$.

Question: $$-2 x+3 y=6$$In the $x y$-plane, the graph of which of the following equations is perpendicular to the graph of the equation above?
Choices:
  A: $3 x+2 y=6$
  B: $3 x+4 y=6$
  C: $2 x+4 y=6$
  D: $2 x+6 y=3$
Response 0:
Thought:
The equation of a line perpendicular to another line has a slope that is the negative reciprocal of the slope of the original line.
The given equation can be rewritten in slope-intercept form as $y=\frac{2}{3}x+2$.
The negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$ is $-\frac{3}{2}$.
Therefore, the equation we are looking for has a slope of $-\frac{3}{2}$.
We can rewrite the answer choices in slope-intercept form to determine which one has a slope of $-\frac{3}{2}$.
A: $3 x+2 y=6 \Rightarrow y=-\frac{3}{2}x+3$
B: $3 x+4 y=6 \Rightarrow y=-\frac{3}{4}x+\frac{3}{4}$
C: $2 x+4 y=6 \Rightarrow y=-\frac{1}{2}x+\frac{3}{2}$
D: $2 x+6 y=3 \Rightarrow y=-\frac{1}{3}x+\frac{1}{2}$
The equation that has a slope of $-\frac{3}{2}$ is A.
Action: Answer("A")

  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5

  Simplifying the expression, we get 5 kilometers (rounded to the nearest kilometer).
  The answer is D: 5.

Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The DBA plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year.
  There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year.
  The function that best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now should take into account the initial number of businesses and the increase in membership per year.
  The function that satisfies these conditions is $y=n x+b$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $y=n x+b$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 98 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$Which of the following represents all the possible values of $x$ that satisfy the equation above?
Choices:
  A: 0 and 2
  B: 0 and 4
  C: -4 and 4
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  Multiply both sides of the equation by $2(x-3)$ to eliminate the denominators.
  Simplify the equation and solve for $x$.
  Check if the solution satisfies the original equation.
  
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Multiply both sides by $2(x-3)$ to eliminate the denominators.
  Simplify the equation and solve for $x$.
  Check if the solution satisfies the original equation.
  
Action: Answer("B") 

Explanation:
  $$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$
  $$2x(x-3)=2(x-3)x$$
  $$2x^2-6x=2x^2-6x$$
  $$0=0$$
  The equation is true for all values of $x$ except $x=3$ (which makes the denominator zero).
  Therefore, the possible values of $x$ are 0 and 4.
  To check:
  $$\frac{0}{0-3}=\frac{2(0)}{2}$$
  $$0=0$$
  $$\frac{4}{4-3}=\frac{2(4)}{2}$$
  $$4=4$$
  Both solutions satisfy the original equation.
Response 2:
Thought:
  Multiply both sides by $2(x-3)$ to eliminate the denominators.
  Simplify the equation and solve for $x$.
  Check if the solution satisfies the original equation.
  
Action: Answer("B")
Response 3:
Thought:
  To solve the equation, we can cross-multiply to get rid of the denominators.
  $$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$
  $$2x(x-3)=2(x)(x-3)$$
  $$2x^2-6x=2x^2-6x$$
  The equation is true for all values of $x$.
  Therefore, the answer is all real numbers.
  The answer is not listed, so we select the most likely answer, which is C: -4 and 4.
Action: Answer("C")

$$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$
$$2x(x-3)=2x(x-3)$$
$$2x^2-6x=2x^2-6x$$
The equation is true for all values of $x$ except for $x=3$ since it would make the denominator of the left-hand side equal to zero. Therefore, the possible values of $x$ that satisfy the equation are all real numbers except for $x=3$.
$$x\in\mathbb{R}, x\neq3$$
The answer is none of the above.

  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$

  Therefore, the answer is C: $-\frac{16}{7}$.

Topic: Math
Question: If $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$, what is the value of $\frac{b}{a} ?$
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4}$
  C: 2
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  Start with $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$.
  Cross-multiply to get $4a = b$.
  Divide both sides by $a$ to get $\frac{b}{a} = \frac{4a}{a} = 4$.
  Therefore, the value of $\frac{b}{a}$ is 4.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We can solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ by isolating the variable on one side of the equation.
  Multiply both sides of the equation by $\frac{b}{2}$ to get rid of the fraction.
  $\frac{2a}{b} \cdot \frac{b}{2} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{b}{2}$
  Simplify the left side of the equation.
  $a = \frac{b}{4}$
  Divide both sides of the equation by $a$ to solve for $\frac{b}{a}$.
  $\frac{a}{a} = \frac{b}{4a}$
  $1 = \frac{b}{4a}$
  Multiply both sides of the equation by $4$.
  $4 = \frac{4b}{4a}$
  Simplify the right side of the equation.
  $4 = \frac{b}{a}$
  Therefore, the value of $\frac{b}{a}$ is 4.
  The answer is D: 4.
Action: Answer("D")

Thought:
  Start with $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$.
  Multiply both sides by $\frac{b}{2}$ to get $a = \frac{b}{4}$.

  Therefore, the answer is D: 4.

  Simplify the left side of the equation.
  $a = \frac{b}{4}$
  Divide both sides of the equation by $a$ to solve for $\frac{b}{a}$.

  $\frac{b}{4a}$
